<Rating>5</Rating>< Review>
This park has lots of space and and a variety of trails to run around on. Everything is fairly spread out rather than one big play structure. The easy climbing wall and rope pyramid are hits with my kids. The water-play feature is unique but the flow rate is a mere trickle. The lack of a dedicated parking lot is the only downside, and that assumes you are driving here.<//Review>

<userid>104001535125942193717< /userid><user_name>Max Rae< /user_name><date>1517796382733<//date><Rate>4<//Rate>< Text>
Love everything about this park... other than a weird tendency for parents to not watch their kids.  Been here dozen times and each time I find myself having to police kids running amuck while parents chat among themselves.  Usually older kids (9-10 yrs old).  And I get that kids that age don't need to be hovered over, but they still need to be monitored.  Today there was a group of 6 girls all climbing in, over and on top of the tube slide... Almost kicking other kids in the face as they came down the slide.  They also left their shoes and socks all scattered around at the bottom of the slide, leaving other kids to trip all over them.  Their moms?  Sitting on the bench taking selfies.  I know there are parents at every park not paying attention, but speaking anecdotally, there seem to be more parents of older kids who are distracted a lot more (or for a longer period of time) than at other parks.  I imagine it's because it's more of a social gathering spot for the grownups too.  Regardless... it gets annoying after awhile.  Regardless of age -- parents need to keep an eye on their kids to make sure they're being responsible and respectful of others at the park.<//Text>

< Text>
This is my personal experience, your mileage may vary.

Be careful with Xfinity or Comcast.....they lure you in with "specials" that expire and then prices jump up quickly.  Reps will promise deals or free stuff that they won't honor.  You can buy your own equipment and don't have to rent theirs which is very expensive.  They almost always overcharged me and when I called them on it, they wouldn't refund the overcharge.

An In Store rep here felt bad because Comcast had overcharge me and promised free content to offset the charges.  When it didn't show up as promised, I went back, she wasn't working that day so I asked for the manager.  The manager wouldn't come out, hid in back but told the rep I was dealing with they would not honor the commitment even though I had it in writing on the rep's business card.  Blew my mind and forever changed my opinion of Comcast...

In Comcasts defense, their internet only is OK as long as you only care about download speeds.  Their service for the most part is limited to much slower upload speeds, mine was capped at 12mbps with 150mbps download.  Before I switched to Sonic fiber which is $90/mo for 1gig up and down, I used Comcast internet and it worked.  I now only pay for internet and stream whatever services I need, i.e. youtubetv, netflix, youtube music, amazonprime etc.

If you have no other choice, Comcast is reliable if a bit confusing and expensive...just be careful.  Always review your statement to make sure you're not paying for something you didn't sign up for or are not being provided..... :-(<//Text>

Did you know you can get your child as young as 10-years old PADI Open Water (Junior) Certified?  A really important question is: should you?

Certifying our son, who just turned 12, didn‚Äôt even occur to my wife and me until we finally booked that dream trip to Australia.  We booked a couple nights on a liveaboard on the Great Barrier Reef.  At first, we planned to just snorkel with him, ‚Äúchase bubbles.‚Äù  Then we found that he could scuba with us.

We can, but should we?  Getting Open Water Certified in South California in Winter is not a trivial pursuit, especially for children who don‚Äôt spend a lot of time in the water.

We researched the local Certification Programs and decided that House of Scuba was the best fit for us.  Their staff was friendly and professional and their shop was well stocked from the value end to the ‚Äúelite‚Äù end of the spectrum.

Kevin, the Shop Manager, was helpful in setting expectations.  We felt comfortable and ready.

Justin, our group‚Äôs Instructor, was without a doubt the best instructor you could hope for.  Certified at 10 or 12 (I forget), he is a True Believer.  More time in the water than out.  He still remembers what it was like to be certified as a child ‚Äì the special challenges ‚Äì since it wasn‚Äôt that long ago.  His demeanor with both the adults and the kids was perfect.  He is professional, extremely knowledgeable, highly-qualified and kept the dives very enjoyable, but properly focused.

So back to certifying your child.  There is a risk of your child not being comfortable with the non-tropical California conditions.  Your child might not be comfortable enough to meet the certification requirements?  Should you try, without knowing for sure if your child is capable?  The answer: yes.  House of Scuba‚Äôs staff and instructors know what they‚Äôre doing, understand the challenges for adults and children, and are very capable of finding solutions.

We had a short window to try to get all the dives in.  Conditions weren‚Äôt optimum. My son had little snorkeling experience.  He had some issues on his second Open Water check dive.

Kevin and Justin recommended finishing the dives with one-on-one instruction.  Having little time, I pushed to finish the dives on the following weekend.  Ocean Conditions were very rough, but the bay can be used as a backup, though visibility is often quite poor.  Though the staff recommended waiting for an Ocean Dive, Kevin and Justin accommodated our request.  This customer is NOT always right‚Ä¶

Our son just wasn‚Äôt comfortable in the bay, so we did not finish the dives.  This was his First Big Fail and it could have been emotionally catastrophic.  Our son‚Äôs disappointment was deep, but Justin‚Äôs professionalism, experience, delicacy and grace throughout the pool and Open Water dives really kept the experience a positive one.  Justin handled everything perfectly.

Back at the shop, everyone was very supportive.  It did not feel like a Fail.  Kevin was outstanding with the business side of things and we are arranging to complete the PADI Certification via Referral in the clear, warm, summer waters of the Great Barrier Reef.  Our son has very good instruction and some pretty substantial experience in far less comfortable conditions; I‚Äôm completely sure that he will be fine and complete his Certification there.

So, back to the question: ‚ÄúI‚Äôm not sure that my kid is capable of getting certified yet. Should we try?‚Äù  I say: yes!

There are a lot of factors that are beyond control; House of Scuba does a really good job with all the factors that are controllable.  They even were able to make our First Big Fail a Temporary Hiccup (and an excellent learning experience).

We‚Äôre disappointed that we did not get certified on schedule, but really happy that we tried and that we chose House of Scuba to help my son get started in this wonderful lifelong adventure.

Followup:  I attended my son's Certification Dives in Australia.  Even though it was two months since the Pool and Ocean Dives with Justin, it was clear that Justin did a great job teaching What, How, and Why.</Text>

< Text>
On-line buyer beware!!  My experience with House of Scuba was purchasing snorkeling masks on-line.  I ordered three masks to try on to find the best fit.  My order qualified for FREE shipping.  Beware, it is only free shipping if you do not return anything.  I found this out when my refund did not match my purchase price.  When I first read the return policy, I saw this -  If it is within 60 days and the items are in new condition with original packaging, there is a 100% credit or refund available on any item.  This led me to believe I would receive a full refund.  But wait, there's more...in the paragraph above it states you will be charged for the amount of free shipping you were originally given on your order.  So in reality it is not FREE shipping after all.  On-line purchasers be aware of this fact.  If I had realized it, I would have chosen to take my business to another website.  After I protested they offered a store credit but that is of no use since I will take my business elsewhere.</Text>

< review>
I recently bought a used Ninja 250r and it quickly got a flat tire. I had it towed to Berkeley Performance Motorcycle for new tires; since it was in the shop anyway, I went ahead and requested a carb clean because it had some issues starting up and would stumble quite a bit after it warmed up -- I just suspected that it was a carb-related issue. Within the next couple business days, Carra contacted me via phone and text to let me know that the tires were put on and that the carb was actually in good condition and needed no work. It turned out that the issue was attributable to some leftover bad gas (an oversight on my part). Carra further informed me of a couple other minor issues that she could take care of, but didn't do anything without my permission. I was impressed by the shop's integrity and would definitely recommend utilizing the services offered.< /review>

< text>
Wow, prices are amazing! Large showroom many different options for those on a budget. When I went I was looking at sectionals and couches for a new apartment. While checking the furniture out a male worker came over and started showing me how different sectionals converted into sleepers. He was very helpful and I appreciated his willingness to show me the functionality of different pieces I was interested in purchasing. He was a lot more knowledgeable than the female European sales person sitting at a desk. The female didn't even know that the store sold adjustable bed frames when I inquired about the beds. I had to correct her and inform her that the store sold more than mattresses. If you go, I'd see if the middle aged Spanish man is available. He can help you with the functions available with the furniture and won't make you feel stupid for asking questions. I'd recommend that you check it out yourself and get blown away with the prices. Happy furniture hunting...< /text>
